    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer6614630133992595127"><b>Bestselling author Kresley Cole continues her seductive Immortals After Dark series with this tale of a vampire shunned even by his own kind and a beautiful phantom, bound together by a passion they cannot resist.</b><br/><br/>A RAVEN-HAIRED TEMPTRESS OF THE DARK...<br/><br/>Néomi Laress, a famous ballerina from a past century, became a phantom the night she was murdered.   <span id="freeText6614630133992595127" style="display:none"><b>Bestselling author Kresley Cole continues her seductive Immortals After Dark series with this tale of a vampire shunned even by his own kind and a beautiful phantom, bound together by a passion they cannot resist.</b><br /><br />A RAVEN-HAIRED TEMPTRESS OF THE DARK...<br /><br />Néomi Laress, a famous ballerina from a past century, became a phantom the night she was murdered. Imbued with otherworldly powers but invisible to the living, she haunts her beloved home, scaring away trespassers -- until she encounters a ruthless immortal even more terrifying than Néomi herself.<br /><br />A VAMPIRE WARRIOR CONSUMED BY MADNESS...<br /><br />To prevent him from harming others, Conrad Wroth's brothers imprison him in an abandoned manor. But there, a female only he can see seems determined to drive him further into madness. The exquisite creature torments him with desire, leaving his body racked with lust and his soul torn as he finds himself coveting her for his own.<br /><br />HOW FAR WILL HE GO TO CLAIM HER?<br /><br />Yet even if Conrad can win Néomi, evil still surrounds her. Once he returns to the brutality of his past to protect her, will he succumb to the dark needs seething inside him?</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1593160517" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9688829491372032833">Keeping with the same pattern of earlier books in the 'Immortals After Dark' series, this fifth book in the series tells the story of another "unblooded" male that meets his mate. This time around, the female is a ghost, Naomi, and the male vampire is Conrad, brother to earlier heroes in the series. <br/><br/>The fact that Naomi doesn't have an actual body for a large part of this story put a different spin on things. At times, I was wondering how in the world Ms. Cole would manage to pull off a love stor</span>
  <span id="freeText9688829491372032833" style="display:none">Keeping with the same pattern of earlier books in the 'Immortals After Dark' series, this fifth book in the series tells the story of another "unblooded" male that meets his mate. This time around, the female is a ghost, Naomi, and the male vampire is Conrad, brother to earlier heroes in the series. <br /><br />The fact that Naomi doesn't have an actual body for a large part of this story put a different spin on things. At times, I was wondering how in the world Ms. Cole would manage to pull off a love story when one of the main characters was little more than air. It certainly made the thought of "blooding" mind-boggling.<br /><br />However, all my concerns were for nothing. These two characters came together beautifully. Like the earlier couples in this series, their chemistry was off the charts! <br /><br />If you love a strong, high-handed, alpha-male hero and an equally tough and sassy heroine, this series doesn't disappoint! I'm hooked on this series. It's on to the next one for me.</span>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer319446388" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3391745035859227526"><b>5 + stars</b><br/><br/><i>Dark Needs at Night's Edge</i> was an absolutely fantastic read! I loved everything about this book. In fact, it might just be my favorite in the series thus far. I could go on and on about what I loved about this story, but I'm very anxious to start the next book in the series to find out what happens to Cade, the demon. <br/><br/>Suffice it to say, this book has everything I love in a paranormal AND in a romance book. It has a creative and compelling world, a fascinating cast of motley characters, </span>
  <span id="freeText3391745035859227526" style="display:none"><b>5 + stars</b><br /><br /><i>Dark Needs at Night's Edge</i> was an absolutely fantastic read! I loved everything about this book. In fact, it might just be my favorite in the series thus far. I could go on and on about what I loved about this story, but I'm very anxious to start the next book in the series to find out what happens to Cade, the demon. <br /><br />Suffice it to say, this book has everything I love in a paranormal AND in a romance book. It has a creative and compelling world, a fascinating cast of motley characters, an endearing and genuine couple, with one heck of an emotional romance. I not only fell in love with the hero, Conrad, and heroine, Néomi, personally, but I fell completely in love with their love story. The overwhelming yearning and desire the hero and heroine had for each other in this book was extremely palatable and written beautifully. <br /><br />Conrad sums this book up perfectly when he said, "My Bride by fate, my wife by choice..." <br /><br /><i>Dark Needs at Night's Edge</i> is another fantastic book in what is proving to be an outstanding series.  <br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_150251254" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/150251254" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/150251254?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=should-have-been-bad">should-have-been-bad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=romance-romance-romance">romance-romance-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer150251254" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6164439925788072170">Dark Needs at Night's Edge is a modern, more intensely paranormal version of The Ghost and Mrs. Muir.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346110i/700590.jpg' alt='Mrs. Muir' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>Rex Harrison: making ghosts sexy since 1947.</i><br/><br/>It is, to date, my absolute favourite book in this series. Not that it's really had that much competition.<br/><br/>So far it stands against an abductor, rapist, Sebastian/Kaderine who rock, and Bowen/Marie who don't.<br/><br/>Conrad, a bloodmad and vicious vampire, is captured by his three brothers and trapped in an old mansion to help recover his sanity. Néomi, a 1920's </span>
  <span id="freeText6164439925788072170" style="display:none">Dark Needs at Night's Edge is a modern, more intensely paranormal version of The Ghost and Mrs. Muir.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346110i/700590.jpg" alt="Mrs. Muir" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Rex Harrison: making ghosts sexy since 1947.</i><br><br>It is, to date, my absolute favourite book in this series. Not that it's really had that much competition.<br><br>So far it stands against an abductor, rapist, Sebastian/Kaderine who rock, and Bowen/Marie who don't.<br><br>Conrad, a bloodmad and vicious vampire, is captured by his three brothers and trapped in an old mansion to help recover his sanity. Néomi, a 1920's Prima Ballerina (and former Burlesque dancer) currently haunts said mansion as this was where she was violently murdered.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380346110i/700591.jpg" alt="Dita" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Burlesque, aye? I like her already!</i><br><br>Of course, the sexually confidant, lively and brazen ghost is the perfect partner for virginal, uptight and angry Conrad. Their seduction and romance is, for most of this novel, based on their attraction to each other and telling each other every little thing they would do if only they could touch. <br><br>Néomi absolutely made this novel for me. She was so confidant in her sexuality, so proud of her achievements, so full of life! Conrad's inability to be the typical alpha male with her was also just SO damn refreshing. He couldn't push her around, bully her or trap her. And when it came to wooing her, he couldn't just take her for a walk on the beach or start kissing her. <br><br>The creepy atmosphere created at the beginning of the novel, as well as the slow burn relationship build between Néomi and Conrad, separates this book from a genre which is all about waiting for the next titty grap or alpha male bullshit that is supposedly romantic.<br><br>This book would have absolutely gotten four stars from me if the ending weren't a little contrived toward HEA. The first 90% of this book was so well written, so romantic, so lovely that I was absolutely enchanted. Spoiled only in the last 10% by Cole bending over backwards to give us a "perfect" ending.<br><br>If you never pick up another Cole novel because you are afraid of the romance industry mainstays of the ultra masculine male and the stockholm syndrome suffering female, then at least feel confidant that with Dark Needs at Night's Edge, Cole did something nicely different.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6164439925788072170" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_300376348" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/300376348" />
    <a title="Exina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5309539-exina"><img alt="Exina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580809437p2/5309539.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/300376348?book_show_action=true">Mar 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Exina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Exina" href="/user/show/5309539-exina">Exina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5309539-exina?shelf=series">series</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer300376348" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5244062880646088770"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Dreams can change."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>I loved this story! After the gruesome prologue there is non-stop action: the plot is thrilling, and so complex, that I don’t even dare to summarize it. Brilliant characterization, incredible sexual tension, and Cole’s hallmark humor make this book unputdownable.<br/><br/>Once both Néomi and Conrad were humans. Néomi became a ghost, Conrad changed to a vampire. Now both of them suffer from being what they are.<br/><br/>In his human life, <b>Conrad</b> was denied any happiness; his change to</span>
  <span id="freeText5244062880646088770" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Dreams can change."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved this story! After the gruesome prologue there is non-stop action: the plot is thrilling, and so complex, that I don’t even dare to summarize it. Brilliant characterization, incredible sexual tension, and Cole’s hallmark humor make this book unputdownable.<br><br>Once both Néomi and Conrad were humans. Néomi became a ghost, Conrad changed to a vampire. Now both of them suffer from being what they are.<br><br>In his human life, <b>Conrad</b> was denied any happiness; his change to a vampire infuriated him, and he became a hitman. He went insane by drinking his victims to death because he attained not only their blood, but their horrible memories as well.<br><br>Now bloodthirst blurs his mind. He is hunted by his enemies, by hallucinations, by horrible memories of his own and his victims’. He desperately runs to his end. He is a man who definitely needs to be saved.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471211204i/20012140._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>On the contrary, <b>Néomi</b> lived a full life; she was a celebrated ballerina. It is so touching that as a ghost she is still filled with exhilaration: she tries to brighten her colorless existence with stolen trinkets, and stolen moments. She is unimaginably lonely, still she has a positive attitude.<br>She is bantering, playful, and I love her delicate sense of humor.<br>Her abilities are remarkable even in this ghostly existence, but by the end of the story she becomes a very, very special being. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471211204i/20012141._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the beginning of the story, Conrad’s insanity is represented by short, staccato sentences in simple present tense. This fragmented style perfectly pictures how unstable he is. At first, he is unable to make a distinction between reality and unreality. He doesn’t know whether Néomi is a delusion, a fractured memory, a hallucination, or a ghost.<br><br>Néomi is incorporeal, so Conrad is forced to behave reasonably and collected if he wants to keep her by his side. It helps him to defeat his insanity. He feels clearer, more focused in her presence. Conrad is intense, morose, feral, but also has a romantic, gentle side.<br><br>The sexual tension is incredible in this novel, since they are incapable of touching each other in the larger part of the story. They get to know each other by talking, teasing, and debating. Waiting and hope give an extra sensation to the story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471211204i/20012142.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Conrad and Néomi’s story is a very original and peculiar installment of the <i>Immortals After Dark </i>series.<br><br><a href="http://exinasreadings.tumblr.com/tagged/Dark-Needs-at-Night%E2%80%99s-Edge" rel="nofollow noopener">My favorite quotes.</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5889593844869664923"><b>Conrad Wroth, Vampire & Naomi Laress, Phantom </b><br/><br/>I am not really a fan of Ghosts in paranormal books – mainly because ghosts have no substance. They are just thin air. Moreover, they are usually stuck in one place. They are not allowed to walk around anywhere else on the Earth. And finally, when there is a ghost, there is also his/her dead body rottening somewhere near. And this is not very appealing.<br/><br/>So, I thought that I wouldn’t like this story: <br/>The story of a really sad ghost and of a crazy from </span>
  <span id="freeText5889593844869664923" style="display:none"><b>Conrad Wroth, Vampire &amp; Naomi Laress, Phantom </b><br /><br />I am not really a fan of Ghosts in paranormal books – mainly because ghosts have no substance. They are just thin air. Moreover, they are usually stuck in one place. They are not allowed to walk around anywhere else on the Earth. And finally, when there is a ghost, there is also his/her dead body rottening somewhere near. And this is not very appealing.<br /><br />So, I thought that I wouldn’t like this story: <br />The story of a really sad ghost and of a crazy from bloodlust vampire. Two tortured creatures, born in different centuries, who were obviously ment to be together. But one could not soothe the other because the ghost was not flesh and blood.<br /><br />When Conrad is chained at the Elancourt manor by the three other Wroth brothers in an attempt to cure him, he thinks that the beautiful woman that keeps visiting him at his bed is just a product of his imagination. He is obviously crazy and starved since his brother do not allow him to take blood from a vein to feed. He didn’t know that ghosts exist.<br /><br />Néomi Laress used to be a famous ballerina full of spirit and life before her ex-fiancé stabbed her and brutally took her life. Now in her house for 80 years, she is just a lonely, miserable ghost until a beautiful, chained vampire (obviously crazy) starts talking to her. She didn’t know that vampires exist.<br /><br />It will be really hard for these two lovers-to-be. They will struggle to accept that:<br />•	Ghosts and Vampires are real<br />•	Néomi is Conrad’s bride<br />•	Conrad has to choose his bride instead of his revenge<br />•	Néomi needs to be have a body to make Conrad’s heart beat again<br /><br />The brothers will help, the witches will help, the valkyries will help. <br />And I just loved the end of the story and the way the author managed to make a ghost really likable and sexy.</span>

  <span id="freeText3923079675045768191" style="display:none"> <b>25th May 2020</b><br />I love it when a book stays fabulous, this book remains a gem and always ensures I finish reading with a smile.<br /><br /> <b>October 30th 2018</b><br />So I'm going through a bit of a re-read phase and I'm glad I did with Dark Need at Night's Edge, which remains one of my favourite Kresley Cole books. <div id="review_35542630" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/35542630" />
    <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"><img alt=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1403239075p2/1570669.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/35542630?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)" href="/user/show/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books"> Danielle The Book Huntress (Back to the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of paranormal romance,  Fans of virgin heroes</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=bad-girl-heroine">bad-girl-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero">scary-sexy-cool-dangerous-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=virgin-hero">virgin-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=bad-boy-rake-or-rogue">bad-boy-rake-or-rogue</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=ghost">ghost</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=hot-and-steamy-romance">hot-and-steamy-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=part-of-a-series">part-of-a-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=fated-to-be-mated">fated-to-be-mated</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer35542630" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11719882650815754611">I had to place my faith in Ms. Cole that this premise of a ghost falling in love with a vampire would work. I just couldn't see how this would go well at all. My faith was rewarded. I loved this book. It starts out so beautiful and even gothic. Neomi Laress is brutally murdered by a spurned lover in her house that she has just bought at a grand party she is throwing to celebrate her retirement from the ballet. She is a beautiful dancer in the early 20th century who has decided to leave her curre</span>
  <span id="freeText11719882650815754611" style="display:none">I had to place my faith in Ms. Cole that this premise of a ghost falling in love with a vampire would work. I just couldn't see how this would go well at all. My faith was rewarded. I loved this book. It starts out so beautiful and even gothic. Neomi Laress is brutally murdered by a spurned lover in her house that she has just bought at a grand party she is throwing to celebrate her retirement from the ballet. She is a beautiful dancer in the early 20th century who has decided to leave her current beau. He stabs her in the heart and kills her. I was like, "Wow." This book already managed to stand out from the previous books, just with the prologue.<br /><br />Things only get better. We meet Conrad, the long-lost Wroth brother. In the first few books you always hear that there are four brothers alive still (or undead rather), but that Conrad ran off, angry that his brothers had turned him into a vampire. Finally we get to see him, and things aren't pretty. He has become a mercenary/assassin and a vampire killer. He kills by taking their blood, thus having given himself over to Bloodlust. He vows to kill his other brothers for what they have made him. Kill them and anyone they love.<br /><br />But fortunately, Nikolai, Murdoch, and Sebastian have not given up on their brother. They manage to capture him and have decided to keep him imprisoned until the Bloodlust wears off. Well, they end up keeping him prisoner in the property owned by the deceased Neomi. Unbeknownst to them, her disembodied spirit is still in her beloved home.<br /><br />Neomi has been alone for so long. There have been people who came and went from her home, leaving her alone again. But none have captivated her like Conrad. Despite his blood-red eyes and his insanity, Neomi is very attracted to the brawny and beautiful vampire. Conrad sees her, which is very unusual, since most of the people who have come through her house cannot.<br /><br />Thus begins the seduction of Conrad by Neomi. Neomi is a sensualist, she loves beautiful men and their bodies. It's the worst sort of torture to be around a beautiful male like Conrad and not be able to touch him. Conrad is a virgin, never having loved or made love to a woman. He sees the beautiful ghost and believes she is part of his raving insanity. With each person he killed by draining them, he absorbed their memories. This drives a vampire insane. Since Conrad killed the worst of all kinds of demons and vampire, he is violently insane. But somehow the beautiful spirit manages to calm his raving madness. He falls for her very quickly, and determines to find a way for them to be together. <br /><br />There are problems with this relationship from the start. He wants to feel the same intense desire for her that she feels for him, but because he is a vampire, he cannot feel desire until he is blooded. He feels in his heart that Neomi must be his bride. However, she's a spirit, so she cannot truly 'blood' him. And even if she could 'blood' him, since she's a ghost, they really couldn't get physical anyway.<br /><br />This story really captivated me. I was so sucked into it, that I remember sitting at dinner trying to eat with one hand and reading the book held in the other. My mother was so curious about my fixation with the book, she ended up reading it herself. <br /><br />I liked the way Ms. Cole turned the tables, making Conrad the innocent (sexually) virgin, and Neomi the seducer. I loved the glimpses into other aspects of the Immortals After Dark universe, the Lore, inhabited by all sorts of immortal creatures. Ms. Cole has a way of making these books laugh-out loud funny, but also intense and poignant. Conrad is the type of hero that gets under your skin and you feel for him. Although Neomi had some hardened aspects to her that I typically don't care for in a heroine, I ended up loving her as well. I loved her intense feelings for Conrad, almost from the start. They weren't just lust, but a sense of ownership like he was dear to her. I also appreciated her passion for life and culture, and how much she loved her home. She had a good heart and was kind to the good people who stopped through her home. So it was easier than I thought to come to like her as heroine. Even though Conrad was insane and technically a murderer (really just of bad creatures), I loved him from the start. Seeing his madness and his loneliness really opened my heart to him. Despite the outer wrappings, you could see a deep sort of innocence in him that was more than just sexual. <br /><br />Even with the obvious issues in their relationship, Conrad and Neomi really came across as soulmates, and very early in this book. I really rooted for this unlikely couple to be together, and the way in which this comes to pass was very well done. I must say, my respect for Ms. Cole as an author went up another notch at how she brought Conrad and Neomi's happy ever after together.<br /><br />Despite my misgivings when I first heard the storyline for this story, I came to love Dark Needs at Night's Edge with the same passion that I loved the prior stories (and possibly more). Conrad was a new favorite hero, at least until Cadeon and Rydstrom came around. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11719882650815754611" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

Even though the plot was a lot different than the other books in the series, I still found this one hard to put down. It just felt so unusual to me, but in a good way. Mad vampire assassin meets lonely, beautiful ballerina ghost and falls in love against all odds--I just wasn't expecting that!   <span id="freeText3064394682396898377" style="display:none">I have to rate this another 5 star read by Kresley Cole. Even though the plot was a lot different than the other books in the series, I still found this one hard to put down. It just felt so unusual to me, but in a good way. Mad vampire assassin meets lonely, beautiful ballerina ghost and falls in love against all odds--I just wasn't expecting that! I loved how Conrad and Neomi 'connected' over their long talks while each was a prisoner inside Neomi's estate. Loved their little game of black jack and answer the question. Loved seeing Conrad's vampire brothers making return appearances. Loved the friendship between Mari and Neomi and Nix. Loved the flirting between the un-schooled Conrad and the more experienced Neomi--it was very sensual. And I especially loved when Conrad was finally 'blooded'--wow! The sex scenes in this book were probably the most erotic of the whole series so far! And Conrad was one romantic hero! I thought the ending was a little far out and at times confusing, but I decided to just go with it and enjoy it, and I did! I'm finding all the characters in this series just terribly sympathetic, and I want them all to have a HEA. Now I can't wait to read the demon Cade's story!</span>

Neomi Laress soul being so strong becomes a ghost, and she has since then become a prisoner in her own home in Elancourt. The bloodthirsty vampire Conrad Wroth gets captured and gets taken away by his brothers to Elancourt to help him heal his madness,and that where no one else can, he starts to see this beautiful woman who soothes his anger and gives him peace. He falls very soon in love with her, and the journey of love between these two,just how powerful it was is something i never could describe.!<br />Neomi Laress is a creature of sensuality who loves dancing,laughter,music and beauty.She is a seductress of her own class and damn well good at it.And i love it how she sees Conrad as "hers" calling him "her vampire" which he also loved,hihi.I could 13-year old kid,killing and surviving is the only thing he have known and was he notorious when it came to it!Ahhh but he is the most unusual Anti-hero of them all with his innocence that didn`t only lie in sexuality,and i so so so came to FALL FOR HIM!How he instantly comes to crave Neomis presence,and how he sulked when she didn`t appear,ADORABLE!She becomes the one and only woman he have ever loved,and how he claims her when she bloodies him,yum!How they connected during their prisonment in the manor,and how they utterly desired each other,their romance came out so strong that my heart nearly bursted with it.They are so beautiful together!And the angst that came out on the impossibility of touch between them made it all so more sensual,Neomi being the one seducing Conrad was so FREAKING HOT!Conrad worshiped the ground she walked on and would be ready to give up his life for her was BEAUTFUL!They are both beautiful together,and with their golden hearts i just whole-heartedly fell in love with them.I will never forget Conrad and Neomi,never,and they are my currently favourite couple right now in this series.My pounding heart!How i love this book,Kresley Cole has again changed my life for the better and i so look forward to read the next book in the series!<br /><br />Raising his bound hands over her head, he again surrounded her with his body. “What if I wanted to         <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer945172557" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3438738760888644213"><b>*****4.0 This Series Rocks Stars*****</b><br/><br/><b>Conrad Wroth</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403089273i/10036172._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='560' alt='Conrad' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The Vampire, Conrad Wroth, is a highly paid assassin. He kills other immortals by drinking their blood until he obtains their power and their memories. But all that killing and drinking has caused Conrad to become consumed with blood lust. And he can no longer distinguish his memories from those of his victims. He's pretty much gone mad.<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403090412i/10036401._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='256' alt='haunted house' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>So his brothers buy an old abandoned property and imprison him in the abandoned manor. And as fate would have it</span>
  <span id="freeText3438738760888644213" style="display:none"><b>*****4.0 This Series Rocks Stars*****</b><br><br><b>Conrad Wroth</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403089273i/10036172._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="560" alt="Conrad" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Vampire, Conrad Wroth, is a highly paid assassin. He kills other immortals by drinking their blood until he obtains their power and their memories. But all that killing and drinking has caused Conrad to become consumed with blood lust. And he can no longer distinguish his memories from those of his victims. He's pretty much gone mad.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403090412i/10036401._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="256" alt="haunted house" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>So his brothers buy an old abandoned property and imprison him in the abandoned manor. And as fate would have it, only Conrad can see the ghost that lives there. His brothers refuse to believe him, thinking he is insane in the membrane!! They fear that they will have to end his life if they are unable to rehabilitate him.<br><br><br><b>Naomi Laress</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402751481i/9982066._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="483" alt="black extension" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Naomi was once a talented ballerina…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402751872i/9982104._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="303" alt="red air split" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She was rich and famous…<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1402751481i/9982067._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="533" alt="fashion" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The epitome of grace…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402752784ra/9982205.gif" width="400" height="203" alt="amazing" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Until a jaded lover killed her DEAD!!!!</b><br><br><br>Now she's a lonely phantom ghost, left to haunt her home for the past eighty years…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403025494ra/10027209.gif" width="400" height="519" alt="ghost" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>There is an immediate attraction between these two that can not be denied. But Naomi knows that her heart will only shatter if she allows herself to fall in love with a vampire that will heal and then move away. <br><br>Conrad is determined to find a way to be with Naomi. He believes that all obstacles can be conquered. He just needs to kill a few more of his enemies before he settles down. He would hate to put his woman's life at risk. And his list of enemies is Looonngg!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403091236i/10036510.gif" width="400" height="267" alt="line" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book started out great (4.25 stars), but started to drag between the 50-60% mark (3 stars). But then it picked up again at 65% and I was physically unable to put it down (5 stars)!!! So I can give this one a solid 4 star!! I also loved that this was the first couple in the series that <u>
  <b>wanted</b>
</u> to be together. They weren't fighting each other, but fighting circumstances.<br><br> I am still digging the PNR world that <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4428.Kresley_Cole" title="Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Kresley Cole</a> has created. The variety is wonderful. Witches, phantoms, werewolves, vampires, valkyrie, and demons. I look forward to the next book which will finally focus on a demon. I love horned demons!! I can't wait!! *squee*<br><br><br><br><b>My Immortals After Dark Reviews:<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945149690" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945169131" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/949584205" rel="nofollow noopener">No Rest for the Wicked</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172183" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172557" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Needs at Night's Edge</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945172787" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dark Desires After Dusk</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/994211489" rel="nofollow noopener">Kiss of a Demon King</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945174408" rel="nofollow noopener">Untouchable</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945178167" rel="nofollow noopener">Pleasure of a Dark Prince</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945180198" rel="nofollow noopener">Demon from the Dark</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/945180215" rel="nofollow noopener">Dreams of a Dark Warrior</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1289048120" rel="nofollow noopener">Lothaire</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1400296552" rel="nofollow noopener">Dark Skye</a></b></span>

<div id="review_125749945" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/125749945" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/125749945?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">paranormal romance fans, fans of a virgin hero</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers">keep-a-spare-pair-of-knickers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=drinks-on-me">drinks-on-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-kresley-cole">author-kresley-cole</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=virgin-heroes">virgin-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=my-hottie-harem">my-hottie-harem</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer125749945" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9727412185711423156">Well, it looks like my high school French class finally paid off in the end! Again, I breezed through this book! Dark Needs at Night’s Edge was such a thrill to read!<br/><br/>To be honest, I was caught off-guard. I don’t usually enjoy ghost stories so I didn’t expect to be so transfixed by Neomi the French prima ballerina. But I was. The prologue is fantastic and once I started, I couldn’t stop! <br/><br/>Murdered by her ex-husband in a bitter rage, Neomi Laress was stabbed to death in her own home after the brigh</span>
  <span id="freeText9727412185711423156" style="display:none">Well, it looks like my high school French class finally paid off in the end! Again, I breezed through this book! Dark Needs at Night’s Edge was such a thrill to read!<br /><br />To be honest, I was caught off-guard. I don’t usually enjoy ghost stories so I didn’t expect to be so transfixed by Neomi the French prima ballerina. But I was. The prologue is fantastic and once I started, I couldn’t stop! <br /><br />Murdered by her ex-husband in a bitter rage, Neomi Laress was stabbed to death in her own home after the brightest moment of her career. Thousands of years after the murder-suicide, Neomi’s spirit still lingers within her beloved home, forever alone and trapped.<br /><br />But when three brothers haul a crazed and murderous madman into her home, Neomi is helpless in her spiritual form. <br /><br />Conrad Wroth is a Fallen vampire with red eyes. He is also a skilled assassin who has succumbed to Bloodlust. In an effort to save their brother, Nikolai, Sebastian, and Murdoch have chained Conrad in the long abandoned Gothic manor for him to recover. But despite Neomi’s fear of having another murderer in her home, she is intrigued by Conrad....Intrigued by Conrad and his phD (and no, I don’t mean the academic credentials. I mean his pretty huge dick!! ;P) It seems that as a ghost our little ballerina has developed mischievous hobbies, like stealing from her tenants and spying on people. As a former seductress, Neomi can’t resist Conrad’s body so she takes her fill when she can, ogling Little Con because she knows he can’t see.<br /> <br />But Conrad CAN see her! And although he’d die to touch a single hair on her head, he can’t because she possesses no body. Cole really lays on the sexual tension in Dark Needs and she does a fantastic job with it! The frustration and need that both characters have for one another is conveyed nicely and it’s believable. That’s tough to pull off but Cole manages it with ease.<br /><br />I also want to mention how bad I felt for these two. The heroine is a ballerina turned ghost and the hero is warlord turned vampire. Both do not like what they have become but they are dealing with the cards that they have been dealt. Even though Con doesn’t try until later on in the book, he does make a pretty miraculous recovery. And even though Neomi is a ghost, she isn’t the sulking and miserable kind that we normally read about. In fact, I’d argue that she has more life in her as a ghost than Conrad did in the beginning. I have to respect her zest for life.<br /><br />I loved the Gothic Horror feel to this book. The harrowing tone was also perfect for Dark Needs and I think, the next time I pick up one of Kresley Cole’s book, I’ll have more faith in her writing. Because so far, she hasn’t disappointed me at all. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9727412185711423156" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer3468450681335857641"><a href='http://imgur.com/PXt6cOm' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><b>3.5 stars</b>.<br/><br/><i>Waitress :</i> Welcome back to the Fetish Cafe. See anything you like tonight?<br/><br/><i>Me :</i> (closing the menu) Not really. Are there any betas on special tonight?<br/><br/><i>Waitress :</i> (smacking gum) Nope. Outta luck. Some Valkyrie came in and purchased our last beta fantasy. She said something about wanting to hold him facedown over a crocodile...<br/><br/><i>Me :</i> How...quaint. (Gathers things)</span>
  <span id="freeText3468450681335857641" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/PXt6cOm" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1446219140i/16766985.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>3.5 stars</b>.<br><br><i>Waitress :</i> Welcome back to the Fetish Cafe. See anything you like tonight?<br><br><i>Me :</i> (closing the menu) Not really. I feel like I've seen all of this before. Alphas who kidnap, Alphas who rescue, Alphas who fight for their women...I'm bored. Are there any betas on special tonight?<br><br><i>Waitress :</i> (smacking gum) Nope. Outta luck. Some Valkyrie came in and purchased our last beta fantasy. She said something about wanting to hold him facedown over a crocodile...<br><br><i>Me :</i> How...quaint. (Gathers things) Well, I guess better luck next time. I guess tonight is Netflix and solo chill.<br><br><i>Waitress :</i> Uh, wait. I think there's a man in the back that you might be interested in.<br><br><i>Me :</i> Oh?<br><br><i>Waitress :</i> You might need to talk with him for a while before he warms up to you. You see, he's not really here of his own volition. <br><br><i>Me :</i> Wait, wait, wait. I don't do forced scenes. That's not my thing. And it's just wrong.<br><br><i>Waitress :</i> I think he could use a friend. That's all I'm saying. And you seem to have nothing better to do...<br><br>Me : What the??? Look, Bit-<br><br><i>Waitress :</i> (cuts me off, irritated) I have other customers. Have a good night. *walks away*<br><br><i>I gather my stuff and walk toward the back entrance, hoping to avoid the rage demon that won't stop hitting on me every time I visit the cafe. Walking down the long hall that leads to the back entrance, I pass a series of rooms. As I pass the last door on the left, I can hear screams coming from the room. "Let me out you bastards!" screams a deep, masculine voice. Chills overtake my body. Something's not right here. The door is closed, but the latch hasn't taken hold. Do I investigate, or do I leave before things get worse?</i><br><br>************************************************************<br><br><i>Dark Needs</i> was a different type of read than the previous books. There was less outside story happening due to the lead characters being stuck in one location. <br><br>In a way, this both helped and hurt the story. The readers got to learn more about Conrad and Neomi. We also got to see the characters connect in a deeper fashion. Those were positives. But I have to admit that the setting took much of the "fun" element away that was present in the previous books. We had just finished a 2 book arc of characters competing in an Amazing Race type of event. There was non-stop action. And then, all of a sudden, the brakes were put on in favor of watching two people tap-dance their way around each other (okay, so Conrad wasn't dancing because he was chained to a bed, and Neomi was ballet dancing because she's a ballerina, but you know what I mean). <br><br>I love ghost stories. There's always been a pull for me with forbidden love, and ghost stories tend to embody that. Never, is it easy for a ghost to be with a human/vampire/wolf, etc. There's always rules in place - often having to do with the fact that the ghost is rarely able to be touched. <br><br>I probably could have done an entire fetish cafe episode just on that. But how could I avoid "hot guy tied to a bed?" Um, hello...right?<br><br>Even us submissives at heart would have a hard time resisting a hot man tied to a bed. Especially if hot man is suffering. I don't know about the rest of you women, but the fantasy of bringing someone back from the brink is a strong pull. Talk about the gratefulness the man would have. *blinks innocently*<br><br>Dammit. I really want to go back and re-write that scene now. I didn't write to this story's full potential. Ah well. Maybe next time.<br><br>I enjoyed <i>Dark Needs</i>, but would have appreciated a few cut scenes with other characters to break up some of the monotony of watching Conrad and Neomi fumble their way back to life (him from the brink of madness, her from...well, death and all that). <br><br>Nix was awesome, as usual. Love that crazy broad.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3468450681335857641" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14266696339700173076"><br/>Just over two weeks ago, while boarding a 'red-eye' flight from Vegas to Toronto, I thought to myself 'I know I won't be able to sleep so why not pick a book that's already on my kindle to make the four hours go by faster' so I chose <b>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark__1_' title='The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark #1) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Warlord Wants Forever</a>
</b> and the rest, as they say, is history.<br/><br/>I've been completely lost in this magical world of <b>Immortals After Dark</b> ever since and can't get enough of it and it's inhabitants! Néomi Laress & Conrad Wroth are the latest couple to steal my hear</span>
  <span id="freeText14266696339700173076" style="display:none"><br>Just over two weeks ago, while boarding a 'red-eye' flight from Vegas to Toronto, I thought to myself 'I know I won't be able to sleep so why not pick a book that's already on my kindle to make the four hours go by faster' so I chose <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6388558.The_Warlord_Wants_Forever__Immortals_After_Dark__1_" title="The Warlord Wants Forever (Immortals After Dark #1) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a>
</b> and the rest, as they say, is history.<br><br>I've been completely lost in this magical world of <b>Immortals After Dark</b> ever since and can't get enough of it and it's inhabitants! Néomi Laress &amp; Conrad Wroth are the latest couple to steal my heart. I don't think I'll ever comprehend how Kresley Cole manages to take a couple of beings and make their story completely <i>
  <b>their own</b>
</i>! This is the 5th book in the series and never once did I feel like I was reading the same story. The way she puts them in their own setting, fighting a different villain, overcoming a different conflict, etc. is absolutely amazing!<br><br>I said this before &amp; I'm happy to repeat myself: after I was finished with book 1, I really didn't care whose story was next because EVERY SINGLE CHARACTER in this series is story worthy and I just <i>KNEW</i> Kresley Cole will deliver with each book and boy did she ever!<br><br>This author is an auto-buy for me for more several reasons:<br><br>1. her ability to deliver a story is TOP NOTCH!<br>2. her heroines are KICK ASS [I've yet to come across one that I wanted to throttle]!<br>3. her male leads are BEYOND!!<br>4. and I'll never get sick of saying this but I LOVE the ever present humor in her stories!!<br><br>If you are a fan of this author, this series is a MUST READ even if you aren't a fan of this genre because if anyone could make you a convert, Kresley Cole definitely can!<br><br>Cheers!<br><br><a href="http://amzn.to/2bKaW2w" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_179358195" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/179358195" />
    <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance"><img alt="When Funmi Met Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572219419p2/5615242.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/179358195?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="When Funmi Met Romance" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance">When Funmi Met Romance</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">IAD Readers, E.V.E.R.Y.B.O.D.Y!!!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=instant-chemistry">instant-chemistry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=summer-11">summer-11</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=ptsd-suffering-scarred-heroes">ptsd-suffering-scarred-heroes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=setting-lousiana">setting-lousiana</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=strong-best-heroines">strong-best-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer179358195" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1013059535887479759"><br/>ReRead: I LOVE THESE BOOKS. This one was so much fun and conrad is sooooooooooooo amazing. I love a good virgin hero<br/><br/><b>5 stars- Favorite IAD book yet</b><br/><br/><b>Gushing Fangirl Thoughts</b><br/><br/>I'm so happy there is a substantial amount of thorough reviews on this book for I'm about to gush over this like a open wound...:P This book was great. Cole wove an amazing story in "Dark Needs a Night's Edge" I found myself aching for these characters. It seriously amazes me how Cole created such a contradiction of a book. This</span>
  <span id="freeText1013059535887479759" style="display:none"><br />ReRead: I LOVE THESE BOOKS. This one was so much fun and conrad is sooooooooooooo amazing. I love a good virgin hero<br /><br /><b>5 stars- Favorite IAD book yet</b><br /><br /><b>Gushing Fangirl Thoughts</b><br /><br />I'm so happy there is a substantial amount of thorough reviews on this book for I'm about to gush over this like a open wound...:P This book was great. Cole wove an amazing story in "Dark Needs a Night's Edge" I found myself aching for these characters. It seriously amazes me how Cole created such a contradiction of a book. This book made me laugh many times as her books do for it was full witty and sly remarks. However, the book was very VERY intense. I actually wasn't able to predict to the tee everything that would happen in this book nor the ways by which the star crossed lovers would stay together. Romance is always predictable, but not this time. I also deeply connected to the characters. I wanted them to be together so bad I could barely contain myself the some 368 pages... Also, this had <b>the most</b> fulfilling ending :)<br /><br /><b>Heroine:Néomi Laress-</b> Where to begin. She was a perfect heroine for me. I have no complaints. She is a ghost that had a truly tragic demise. The way she dies was cruel and torturous. When I read that scene, I mulled sadly over the atrocities that we humans commit to one another. Murdered in her home, she became tethered to her estate unable to leave. Despite this cruel fate, She is not some embittered hardened maid. Instead, she is full of vivacity and a zest for life. She truly has a love of life, for it was stripped so early and harshly from her. So many writers to try to create heroines that are "lonely." "oh im so lonely in this house full of people" "Daddy pays me no attention I am so very lonely" I've read it time and time again in Romance. However, Kresley Cole actually created a veritable lonely heroine in this book. It was hauntingly sad the way Neomi was destined to spend her life, bound to a house she was murdered in with no interaction. She was PERFECT for hero. <br /><b>Hero:Conrad Wroth</b>- Wow what a man. Conrad Wroth is a vampire and a red eyed, bloodlusting, horde ceding one at that. He has succumbed to bloodlust do to drinking his victims to death. However, i want to point out that the killing isn't as mindless as it seems for he is a mercenary. It is mentioned in the book that he never killed woman, children, and everyone he killed was a bad person...thus them having bounties on them. He has 3 other brothers, Nikolai, Sebastian, and Murdoch. These brothers should be familiar to you if you are reading this in correct order, I must confess I read this in order of interest not chronologically ( it is fun trying to piece this crazy Lore world together out of order =^_^= )Going against their leader, they capture and lock up Conrad in hopes of getting him to recover from this crazy bloodlust. Conrad is horribly thirsty, gets enraged by literally everything, and has consumed all the memories of the people he has killed. The memories thing is really the kicker. Conrad killed rapists, and murderers, and torturers. He is constantly seeing and hearing the abhorrent actions of the porcine filth he killed. I loved Conrad. He is a proud and strong man, so very strong. He has so much pride but his ability to lay it on the line with out any hesitation for what he fights for his beyond commendable. His life has been shrouded in complete loneliness. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[At the age of 13, he joined a force that killed vampires...requiring him to swear fidelity. Well, at about 35, he ended up getting turned into a vampire.If you don't know, being a Vampire means you have no sexual stimulation until you meet your <i>Bride</i> and she <i>bloods</i> you-giving you a heartbeat, breath, and sexual stimulation <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> After being turned, he ran away from everyone and ended up succumbing to bloodlust. He has lived his life bereft of soft feelings, love, and care, all were replaced with constant warfare. Neomi Changed that however...<br /><br /><b>.Neomi and Conrad:</b> This couple is amazing together. They both have endured such heartbreaking loneliness. They are able to heal each other like no other for they alone understand the stark pain of each other's pain. It is deeper than a love match. Its a pain match too, for both of their pain is one in the same as they fight for lucidity. It was so poignant how they interacted while Neomi was unable to feel anything as was Conrad unable to feel her (reminder: She's a ghost :[ ). They had to connect on levels beyond the tangible. By omitting the physical, Kresley allowed me to easily see and believe in the relationship of Neomi and Conrad that surpassed the tangible boundaries. It literally surpassed life as two different variants of immortality were intermingled. I was so happy to finally read a book where the male did not have to show his mate that he was the one through physical prowess. Conrad literally scoured the earth, fought life and death as we know it to get back his Neomi. He embodied desperation as he fought for the only thing in his life worth fighting for. This couple was so perfect and ill fated my stomach was in knots reading this one.<br /><br /><b>overall...</b><br />I know that this review might make the book sound too somber, but please don't take it that way. The book is highly emotional however, Kresley perfect places the scenes as to not overload the reader. For that, I thank her. The ending is SO FREAKING HAPPY. WARNING THIS IS NO SIMPLE SPOILER. THIS IS THE SPOILER OF ALL SPOILERS! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ all i can say is there future is so happy. Kids!! and happiness. Their prophesied future made me cry a little. Im begging for a little ending epilogue on this couple after the series is over so i can read about this family. The best IAD HEA evaaaaa! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> YOU HAVE TO READ THIS BOOK!!! I loved it and will read it again, and again. </span>
  <a data-text-id="1013059535887479759" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_97323010" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/97323010" />
    <a title="DarienMoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3069494-darienmoya"><img alt="DarienMoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536718485p2/3069494.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/97323010?book_show_action=true">Apr 06, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="DarienMoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="DarienMoya" href="/user/show/3069494-darienmoya">DarienMoya</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3069494-darienmoya?shelf=2010-reads">2010-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3069494-darienmoya?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer97323010" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14892092590417491563">BAD BOY, BAD BOY, WHAT YOU GONNA DO WHEN THEY COME FOR YOU!!!<br/><br/>This is the fourth book in the Immortals After Dark series and this series seems to be getting better. So each book tells you the story of a powerful supernatural male and his fight to win his mate and let me tell you there are fights. Easily this book was the most emotional for me so far and very unconventional with the ending and the love story between the two main characters.<br/><br/>Conrad Wroth is feared and he is hated, but no one could h</span>
  <span id="freeText14892092590417491563" style="display:none">BAD BOY, BAD BOY, WHAT YOU GONNA DO WHEN THEY COME FOR YOU!!!<br /><br />This is the fourth book in the Immortals After Dark series and this series seems to be getting better. So each book tells you the story of a powerful supernatural male and his fight to win his mate and let me tell you there are fights. Easily this book was the most emotional for me so far and very unconventional with the ending and the love story between the two main characters.<br /><br />Conrad Wroth is feared and he is hated, but no one could hate him as much as he hates himself. He is a vampire and they aren’t well liked and even more so for Conrad, he is red eye vampire which makes him dangerous and a whole lot of crazy. You see Conrad drinks directly from his victims then he kills them and when you take blood directly from the source you get all their memories. The things he kill aren’t your upstanding supernatural beings he kills evil demons and other vampires etc, so to walk around with their memories this means that Conrad is a ticking time bomb. He has no sense of reality, days and time have no meaning to him its like he lives in an altered universe where everyone is a potential enemy and in his case they might actually be. Hell bent on destroying everything even his brothers, but faith is about to set in and the brothers he wanted to destroy, are the ones who will bring his salvation and lead him to his Bride.<br /><br />Neomi Laress once a famous ballerina loving her success; and boom ex-fiancé aka crazy plunges a knife into her chest, and just like that dead. Trapped in the home she took her last breath in, now a ghost bored out of her mind and she is one bored ghost all she wants is a permanent resident to reside in the home she loved. The resident she gets is hell bent and destroying her home but she cant help but be drawn into his wild and crazy red eyes. A crazy vampire; but she cant help being drawn to him wanting to tame the crazy beast inside of him. The more reason to want him around is that he can see her, he can even speak with her something that has been impossible in the 80years since her death. Seems though Conrad aka Extreme Crazy is trying to ignore her but Neomi has ways to grab a mans attention even in ghost form.<br /><br />Conrad is falling for the ghost, she is everything he wants in a woman and life just seems a lot more normal when she is around. She relaxes his mind and soothes his hunger to kill. If only there was a way to resurrect her then she could bring his unbeating heart to life and with her he will take his first breath in 300years. Neomi wishes she could be corporeal for the vampire she has grown to love, in this she would give anything. So it begins a love that seems that will only end in destruction will melt your heart. They will have many a obstacles to overcome because Conrad is hated and now he has someone that he cares about, loving him comes with a price. <br /><br />I have to say I loved Conrad, your heart will go out to him. He is so honest with his feelings whether its hating or loving you. Plus he’s funny in a straight jacket and white padded walls sort of way. I liked him and the ghost together, not a normal relationship which makes it spicy. Overall a fun and interesting read with wicked and delicious characters. Kelsey Cole does not disappoint. Its still raining candy in this one and you need to stop by the candy store.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14892092590417491563" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1103482317" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1103482317" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103482317?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/16110517-dark-needs-at-night-s-edge">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2015">audio-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103482317" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10327013680003160263"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/04/audiobook-review-dark-needs-at-nights-edge-by-kresley-cole.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>I strongly suspected that this installment was going to be a miss for me because ghost romances are a personal pet peeve of mine, but I’m listening to this series in order, and it was next up on my to-do list. Kresley Cole’s writing and Robert Petkoff’s narration were by no means at fault here; I still enjoyed many of the secondary elements of this story, the most noteworthy of which being Nix’s dialogue and the author’s phone sex style approach to the earlier love scene</span>
  <span id="freeText10327013680003160263" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/04/audiobook-review-dark-needs-at-nights-edge-by-kresley-cole.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />I strongly suspected that this installment was going to be a miss for me because ghost romances are a personal pet peeve of mine, but I’m listening to this series in order, and it was next up on my to-do list. Kresley Cole’s writing and Robert Petkoff’s narration were by no means at fault here; I still enjoyed many of the secondary elements of this story, the most noteworthy of which being Nix’s dialogue and the author’s phone sex style approach to the earlier love scenes was as erotic as it sounds.<br /><br />Spooks have their place in paranormal fiction such as hauntings, or sidekicks, my difficulty with them lies in their feasibility as happily-ever-after candidates. There are really only two possible scenarios in this type of situation, and that is for either the deceased half of the couple to be revived by magical means, or for the living partner to join their beloved in the beyond. Option two is kind of a downer, so authors tend to ostracize it in favour of the former which essentially means that a character will be brought back to life thus breaking one of my top three hard no-no rules. Again, this is an individual preference.<br /><br />Docking an audiobook two stars for the above seems pretty harsh which is why my quibbles with DARK NEEDS AT A NIGHT’S EDGE do not end there. Initially I liked Conrad’s character; he was edgy, on the cusp of madness, and cutthroat to the extreme. Néomi for her part didn’t make much of an impression on me; she was moody, superficial, and rather boring to be honest. Their relationship was comprised of numerous long winded discussions, stop-and-starts, and overall they just lacked chemistry. I enjoyed the other two Wroth brothers, Bowen, Cadeon &amp; Rydstrom’s brief cameos, and as usual the Soothsayer bits were a slam dunk.<br /><br />I thanked my lucky stars that Robert Petkoff’s narration was there to see my through book 4 because without him I would have been in real danger of giving up on this installment. His transition from present to past tense as he followed Conrad’s progression from insanity to lucidity was a stroke of genius in both its delivery, and Cole’s writing technique. Petkoff stayed true to the French language with his accent, and pronunciations while also conveying Néomi’s coquettish femininity which demonstrated great range considering his aptitude with the bestial alpha males of this series.<br /><br />My issues with DARK NEEDS AT A NIGHT’S EDGE were wholly my own, so what was only an average listen for me could be, and is an extraordinary addition to the IMMORTALS AFTER DARK franchise for the masses.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10327013680003160263" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer452651827" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11157243139155378985">★★★★★ (This is a review of the audio book.) What can I say about hearing one of my favorite installments of Kresley Cole’s wonderful <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series brought to life on audio book? Terrific? Wonderful? Awesome?<br/><br/>They all seem woefully inadequate.<br/><br/>I’ve read this book several times, and I loved listening to it. <b>Robert Petkoff</b> continues his breathtaking narration, kicking it up a notch this time to tell us of Néomi Laress and Conrad Wroth’s love story. His voice is dreamy and he does the in</span>
  <span id="freeText11157243139155378985" style="display:none">★★★★★ (This is a review of the audio book.) What can I say about hearing one of my favorite installments of Kresley Cole’s wonderful <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series brought to life on audio book? Terrific? Wonderful? Awesome?<br /><br />They all seem woefully inadequate.<br /><br />I’ve read this book several times, and I loved listening to it. <b>Robert Petkoff</b> continues his breathtaking narration, kicking it up a notch this time to tell us of Néomi Laress and Conrad Wroth’s love story. His voice is dreamy and he does the international cast of characters wonderfully, maintaining differentiation. His French Quarter accent for Néomi and Estonian accent for Conrad are great...nevertheless, I loved his Nïx the best! She, the “Ever-Knowing” soothsayer, is perplexed in this one and Mr. Petkoff has her inflection – with just the right touch of arrogant attitude thrown in – down perfect.<br /><br />At the beginning one is inclined to wonder how Ms. Cole will ever get these two together. Néomi is not just a former femme fatale and burlesque dancer who rose above her roots to become a prima ballerina of the jazz era, she is a ghost! Worse yet, Conrad is not just a vampire, but one of the “Fallen vampires” and a master assassin. …Oh…and his is just on the edge of insane.<br /><br />Talk about obstacles!<br /><br />Not to mention, Conrad’s brothers have imprisoned him in Elancourt, Néomi’s abandoned New Orleans manor, in order to rid him of his insanity and bloodlust. They can’t see Néomi, so they believe he is not improving, but <i>really</i> losing it. <br /><br />Still, despite the rage and madness, Conrad, the youngest of the Wroth brothers, manages to come across on the pages as… ** whew…fans self**…H.O.T.! I had forgotten how overpowering, demanding, possessive, and relentless he is in his desire for Néomi. I'm not as much of an alpha-hero lover as some of my GoodReads friends, but this one definitely works for me. The love scenes are sizzling. Yet so much of it is – at least in the beginning – cerebral. <br /><br />I don’t want to give the whole story away; however, there are parts of this account that are just plain poignant. Ms. Cole has taken traditional things that we know about and written a wonderful Paranormal-Romance that is truly original. All the while continuing to interweave other characters’ story-lines without the reader getting frustrated by too little or too much information. Fabulous!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11157243139155378985" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4109099687474694891">Book 5 in the series was disappointing for me. Book 4 was so good I was expecting something along the same lines or better.   <span id="freeText4109099687474694891" style="display:none">Book 5 in the series was disappointing for me. Book 4 was so good I was expecting something along the same lines or better. I didn't feel much attraction between Néomi and Connor and when they did finally come together it was anticlimactic. It took so long for something to happen that when it did it fell flat. Something didn't click to make me believe that they really wanted each other the way the other couples in the previous books did. It was a strange kind of tension. I didn't like how she would leave Connor for days and be all pouty when she met up with him again. Connor had potential but he never really shone. <br /><br />Mariketa turns up again in this story but she's a totally different person--very annoying and irritating when she wasn't like that at all in book 4. Bowen, her hubby, makes an appearance and he's good --too bad it's so brief.<br /><br />Hopefully book 6 is better.<br /><br /></span>
