<div id="review_578908369" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578908369" />
    <a title="Angela" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4255477-angela"><img alt="Angela" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398251387p2/4255477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/578908369?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela" href="/user/show/4255477-angela">Angela</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8136398-dark-needs-at-night-s-edge">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2016-read">2016-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4255477-angela?shelf=2019-read">2019-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578908369" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2720472955861712752">June 2019 Re-read.<br/><br/>Erm. Well, we started this buddy read in 2014....and I've let it languish. Time to get going on it again. So, here I am catch up with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1065679506' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sarah</a> ;)<br/><br/>Book 1: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/122560174' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Warlord Wants Forever</a><br/>Book 2: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578909308' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Hunger Like No Other</a><br/>Book 3: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578909438' rel='nofollow noopener'>No Rest for the Wicked</a><br/>Book 4: <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578908664' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a><br/><br/>I gave this three-stars before, apparently, but I think I was being generous then - because I hated this book for the longest time. The first time I read it, was on a cross-country flight. I had nothing else</span>
  <span id="freeText2720472955861712752" style="display:none">June 2019 Re-read.<br /><br />Erm. Well, we started this buddy read in 2014....and I've let it languish. Time to get going on it again. So, here I am catch up with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1065679506" rel="nofollow noopener">Sarah</a> ;)<br /><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/122560174" rel="nofollow noopener">The Warlord Wants Forever</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578909308" rel="nofollow noopener">A Hunger Like No Other</a><br />Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578909438" rel="nofollow noopener">No Rest for the Wicked</a><br />Book 4: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578908664" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Deeds on a Winter's Night</a><br /><br />I gave this three-stars before, apparently, but I think I was being generous then - because I hated this book for the longest time. The first time I read it, was on a cross-country flight. I had nothing else to read, and nothing else to do for the entirety of the flight. I wasn't in the mood for it, and felt that way from the moment I opened the book. But what else could I do? I hate sleeping on flights. So, I forced myself to read it. And it was, I think, that forced reading that made me hate it so much. I couldn't stand anything about the story. Not Conrad, not Neomi, not the love story, nothing. Except maybe Nix. 1-star for Nix, that's what it <i>should</i> have been previously rated.<br /><br />I'd tried re-reading it a few times prior to this massive re-read with Sarah, and each time I got bored a couple of pages in and gave up, skipping directly to the next book. Happily, this re-read has improved my opinion quite a lot. I'd give it a solid 3-stars now. It's still not my favorite of the series, and probably one of my lower-favorites, but it's <i>good</i>. <br /><br />Neomi's an awesome character. Despite the fact that she's a ghost and has been for eighty-some-odd years, she's strong. She was always ahead of her time, independent, wealthy, smart, and confident. I think that she's amazing. I didn't always love how much she capitulated to Conrad's angers and rages, but she also forced herself not to value herself as less, too. She took her fate into her own hands, and made herself - just as she had in life. I truly appreciated that about her character.<br /><br />Conrad, well, he was the biggest problem that I had with the book initially. And don't get me wrong - all the characters in these books can be assholish, so it's not just that he was an ass. I do get why he reacted the way he did quite frequently, it makes sense with his history, and his training, and then the madness; a very real thing for him with all his victims' memories floating around in his head. And I even liked his single-minded approach to setting his goals, and removing the obstacles to those goals from his path. I just never really fell for him. This is probably a hold-over from my first reading (first impressions do stick), so I won't try to hold it against him too much. The other part of the problem is that the vampires are probably my least favorite part of the Lore in this series. There's just so many more interesting factions and groups to be with!<br /><br />I've talked about the world, and plot/pacing of these books at length in my previous reviews - and I think I'd just mostly be repeating myself if I extoled about them again here. But I will say that I continue to be awed at the way that Kresley Cole has interwoven all these storylines and characters and plot-lines. It's truly amazing. There's a plot here that's been brewing for a few books already and doesn't come to fruition for a few books on yet. There are mentions of things happening off page, that we only truly learn about later. This is absolutely my favorite part of this series. It's so tightly woven and created that I've never - in all my years of re-reading it - caught a timeline, or consistency error. And when you're talking about this many characters and things going on and this long of a series .... that's impressive.<br /><br />I can't wait to go onto the next book, because some of my favorites are coming up.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2720472955861712752" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1597760977" />
    <a title="Lisa Kay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay"><img alt="Lisa Kay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1534570690p2/2459470.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1597760977?book_show_action=true">Apr 01, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa Kay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa Kay" href="/user/show/2459470-lisa-kay">Lisa Kay</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/29758369-dark-needs-at-night-s-edge">review of another edition</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=genre-romance-paranormal">genre-romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=reviewed-by-me">reviewed-by-me</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1597760977" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1515262662401062367"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1459561976p8/1415372.jpg' height='250' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>★★★★★ (This is a review of the audio book.) What can I say about hearing one of my favorite installments of Kresley Cole’s wonderful <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series brought to life on audio book? Terrific? Wonderful? Awesome?<br/><br/>They all seem woefully inadequate.<br/><br/>I’ve read this book several times, and I loved listening to it. <b>Robert Petkoff</b> continues his breathtaking narration, kicking it up a notch this time to tell us of Néomi Laress and Conrad Wroth’s love story. His voice is dreamy and he does the in</span>
  <span id="freeText1515262662401062367" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1459561976p8/1415372.jpg" height="250" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>★★★★★ (This is a review of the audio book.) What can I say about hearing one of my favorite installments of Kresley Cole’s wonderful <i>Immortals After Dark</i> series brought to life on audio book? Terrific? Wonderful? Awesome?<br><br>They all seem woefully inadequate.<br><br>I’ve read this book several times, and I loved listening to it. <b>Robert Petkoff</b> continues his breathtaking narration, kicking it up a notch this time to tell us of Néomi Laress and Conrad Wroth’s love story. His voice is dreamy and he does the international cast of characters wonderfully, maintaining differentiation. His French Quarter accent for Néomi and Estonian accent for Conrad are great...nevertheless, I loved his Nïx the best! She, the “Ever-Knowing” soothsayer, is perplexed in this one and Mr. Petkoff has her inflection – with just the right touch of arrogant attitude thrown in – down perfect.<br><br>At the beginning one is inclined to wonder how Ms. Cole will ever get these two together. Néomi is not just a former femme fatale and burlesque dancer who rose above her roots to become a prima ballerina of the jazz era, she is a ghost! Worse yet, Conrad is not just a vampire, but one of the “Fallen vampires” and a master assassin. …Oh…and his is just on the edge of insane.<br><br>Talk about obstacles!<br><br>Not to mention, Conrad’s brothers have imprisoned him in Elancourt, Néomi’s abandoned New Orleans manor, in order to rid him of his insanity and bloodlust. They can’t see Néomi, so they believe he is not improving, but <i>really</i> losing it. <br><br>Still, despite the rage and madness, Conrad, the youngest of the Wroth brothers, manages to come across on the pages as… ** whew…fans self**…H.O.T.! I had forgotten how overpowering, demanding, possessive, and relentless he is in his desire for Néomi. I'm not as much of an alpha-hero lover as some of my GoodReads friends, but this one definitely works for me. The love scenes are sizzling. Yet so much of it is – at least in the beginning – cerebral. <br><br>I don’t want to give the whole story away; however, there are parts of this account that are just plain poignant. Ms. Cole has taken traditional things that we know about and written a wonderful Paranormal-Romance that is truly original. All the while continuing to interweave other characters’ story-lines without the reader getting frustrated by too little or too much information. Fabulous!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1515262662401062367" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_69537577" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/69537577" />
    <a title="Fani *loves angst*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1133802-fani-loves-angst"><img alt="Fani *loves angst*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398440418p2/1133802.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/69537577?book_show_action=true">Aug 31, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fani *loves angst*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fani *loves angst*" href="/user/show/1133802-fani-loves-angst">Fani *loves angst*</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=bad-bad-boy">bad-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=starcrossed-lovers">starcrossed-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=romance-pnr">romance-pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=angsty">angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=social-pariah">social-pariah</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=heroine-i-loved">heroine-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1133802-fani-loves-angst?shelf=assassin-mercenary">assassin-mercenary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer69537577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7018752358773600627">Even when I didn't like the hero, I couldn't put this book down. When I started warming towards him... well, it became a winner! <br/><br/>Connor is a vampire, but one with those dreaded red eyes: that means he drinks from the flesh. And on top of that, he is a hired assasin. After so many years of bloodlust, he's almost mad. The memories he gathered from his victims run without control in his mind so he can't tell if what he's seeing is actually true, a hallucination brought by his fragmented mind or a m</span>
  <span id="freeText7018752358773600627" style="display:none">Even when I didn't like the hero, I couldn't put this book down. When I started warming towards him... well, it became a winner! <br /><br />Connor is a vampire, but one with those dreaded red eyes: that means he drinks from the flesh. And on top of that, he is a hired assasin. After so many years of bloodlust, he's almost mad. The memories he gathered from his victims run without control in his mind so he can't tell if what he's seeing is actually true, a hallucination brought by his fragmented mind or a memory from someone he's killed. And when his brothers capture him trying to cure him out of his bloodlust, he's the only one who sees a beautiful female ghost. So he guesses it's probably a hallucination or past memory. When the ghost starts to interract with him, he can't pretend to ignore her anymore, especially since he finds himself attracted to her. But she isn't corporeal and he isn't blooded, so what chances do they have? Besides, there are a lot of creatures out there trying to kill him and he has to remove the most imminent threat -an 8 inches tall demon- right away, if he wants to have any kind of future with Neomi.<br /><br />I liked fun loving Neomi very much. She was a woman who loved life and enjoyed it to its fullest. I think she was the perfect match for a man like dark, moody man like Connor. I liked the way they got to talk and know each other, their interest turning to mutual attraction and much later to love. Even when they couldn't make love, you could feel the sparks flying between them when they were together:) <br /><br />I don't particularly like Nix's crazyness, nor the Lore's females' mania with food delicacies and soap operas. In fact I get increasingly frustrated at such scenes, rather than amused, but luckily there were too few in this one compared to previous books. I hope there's even less in the future.<br /><br />Heading straight to Cadeon's book. Can't wait to see what Cole has in store for him:)</span>
  <a data-text-id="7018752358773600627" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText7188360631636968016" style="display:none"><b>Reread Review August 6, 2017</b><br /><br />5 "Haunting" Stars!!<br /><br />Best ghost story ever! Like I said with the previous book's reread review, I used to be tough. This one is getting an upgrade to 5 stars too. <br /><br />Conrad was one of the best damaged males ever! He was so very messed up and so very sweet and romantic. He had a raw vulnerability that I just fell hard for. I wanted him healed. I wanted him happy. Naomi! When I grow up, I want to be as sexy, sensual and confident as she was. She knew how to handle her vampire. In all ways, not just in the bedroom.<br /><br />The ending was practically perfect. Though I'll admit predictable. The journey to get there was so good. I could see this one as a movie. <br />There could be some good CGI. Onward IAD reread! Happy reading!!<br /><br /><b>Original Review May 2013</b><br /><br />Really it's 4+ stars! My favorite of the series so far. Conrad is so romantic! The ending is perfect. I highly recommend this one. Happy reading!</span>

<div id="review_265406081" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/265406081" />
    <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox"><img alt="Alex is The Romance Fox" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1428866380p2/6663962.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/265406081?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex is The Romance Fox" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex is The Romance Fox" href="/user/show/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox">Alex is The Romance Fox</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=authors-a-h">authors-a-h</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=humour">humour</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=romance-reading-challenge-2012">romance-reading-challenge-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=sherrilyn-kenyon">sherrilyn-kenyon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=vampire-shapeshifters">vampire-shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6663962-alex-is-the-romance-fox?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer265406081" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15573968660019508507">Kresley Cole -What an incredible storyteller and talented and unique writer you are!!!!!<br/>Her Immortals after Dark Series is beyond amazing….the world of Lore inhabited by such different and varied characters that we have come to know from the previous books is so creatively written , they come alive and are so real and believable that has you engaging in their lives. <br/><br/>I am not crazy about ghost stories and at first had some doubts about this book. Well, after the first two chapters………I was in heav</span>
  <span id="freeText15573968660019508507" style="display:none">Kresley Cole -What an incredible storyteller and talented and unique writer you are!!!!!<br />Her Immortals after Dark Series is beyond amazing….the world of Lore inhabited by such different and varied characters that we have come to know from the previous books is so creatively written , they come alive and are so real and believable that has you engaging in their lives. <br /><br />I am not crazy about ghost stories and at first had some doubts about this book. Well, after the first two chapters………I was in heaven!!!!!!!!!!<br /><br />A turned vampire crazed warrior, with a lost mind and a ghost ballerina who has no body!!!! How will this work out, I wondered. Well, it does – and all because of the magic the author weaves into this so sweet and lovable story of Conrad Wroth and Neomi Laress…<br /><br />I am not going to say much about the plot as parts of the storyline have been written in previous reviews – what was it about this book that made it such a fabulous and more than enjoyable read.<br /><br />CHARACTERS - How Conrad, so dark and driven mad by what he had become and his struggle to overcome his inner demons and how someone like Neomi, filled with sadness and loneliness, longing to find a way to be able to be human again and how her sweet and lovely and caring attitude contributes so much to Conrad’s healing and coming back to what he was before he had become a vampire assassin and reconnecting with his brothers, who had long been lost to him. <br /><br />Somehow, we begin to sympathize with this crazed villain that he was in the beginning and wanting the two to finding a way to be together. <br /><br />Neomi is such a lovable and endearing character. Her mix of French and English is so cute and her whole personality was so enchanting. Loved the way she saw the goodness in Conrad’s heart. Felt her desolation and loneliness ….she just pulls at your heartstrings!!!!<br /><br />The character development is absolutely so well written.<br /><br />Bringing in characters from previous stories is an added bonus!!!! Having met the Valkyrian women, who I am fascinated by – who could not be….they are funny, independent, sexy, magical and unforgettable…you have a sense that you are part of this growing family of demons, werewolves….and waiting expectantly to know who will be next to join this more than amazing Lore family.<br /><br />DIALOGUE – This is one of the things I so love about this series. So much clever wit, funny moments that just works for me…….I know that I will have a smile on my face, laughing my head off when reading anything by Kresley Cole.<br />Here are some of my favorite scenes that really had me “shrieking”<br /><br />Conrad &amp; Neomi are playing twenty rounds of vingt-et-une and the loser has to answers questions about themselves….<br />Conrad – “You weren’t a virgin, were you?”<br />Neomi – “Non, je suis Capricorne!”<br /><br />Marieketa, the witch is using some magic to try and get Neomi a body…..<br />N- “You’ve never attempted it?”<br />M- “On a human? Not outsider a simulator.” After a hesitation, she admitted, “I did recently attempt it on my ghost cat.”<br />N- “And”<br />M- And, did you ever see Pet Sematary?”<br />Neomi shook her head.<br />M- “No? Well, my Tigger came back wrong”, she cried biting her knuckle.<br /><br />Marieketa &amp; Neomi are having a girl’s chat over the fone - tells Neomi she can’t come over and visit because……….<br />“We’re hazing new witches at the coven house today. The innocent lambs are vying for my old room.” She plopped into a cushy chair. “We’ll have to teleconference via mirror”.<br /><br />Marieketa is trying to help Conrad to bringing Neomi back to LIFE……….<br />M- “Oh snap! Live and learn eh? Okay, one vampire’s Bride brought back from the grave.” She slapped her gloved hands and rubbed them together. “Let’s put the fun back in funeral!”<br /><br />THE PLOT – clever, intriguing, different, believable with some surprising twists.<br /><br />SEX SCENES – Tension builds up between Conrad &amp; Neomi’s not being able to touch each other…don’t forget, she’s a ghost….but when it eventually happens…wow….stars explode, fire burns….sensuality at its highest….remember…Neomi is well-versed in the art of love and how lovely it was when she shows Conrad the “ropes” – he’s one hell of a lovable virgin!!!! Eroticism abounds between the pages!!!!! <br /><br />So, finally do these two lovable and enchanting duo get their well-deserved HEA?? Of course they did!!! After all, love always WINS in the end!!!!!<br /><br />Kresley Cole, you rock!!!!!!!!! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15573968660019508507" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1228896409" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2164082033793561613"><b>4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>At first I was like<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389924353ra/8100041.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Soon I thought things started to get interesting.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426985671ra/14153915.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Then I was like<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418738ra/829428.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>By the halfway mark and through the rest of the book I wanted to do this<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383326113ra/6504484.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>A vampire that suffers from bloodlust and has been turned into a killer. Cold and angry at the whole world, he hates himself and all the creatures that are like him. He cannot be sexually stimulated until he finds his bride and is blooded. And when he finally finds her, she cannot blood him because she's not technically alive.<br/><br/>A ghost </span>
  <span id="freeText2164082033793561613" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars</b><br><br>At first I was like<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389924353ra/8100041.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Soon I thought things started to get interesting.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426985671ra/14153915.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Then I was like<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418738ra/829428.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>By the halfway mark and through the rest of the book I wanted to do this<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383326113ra/6504484.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A vampire that suffers from bloodlust and has been turned into a killer. Cold and angry at the whole world, he hates himself and all the creatures that are like him. He cannot be sexually stimulated until he finds his bride and is blooded. And when he finally finds her, she cannot blood him because she's not technically alive.<br><br>A ghost that has been brutally murdered and has lived in solitude for 80 years. She has no corporeal form and though she's started falling in love with her vampire with the red eyes they can never be together physically. A woman that used to love to laugh, socialise and feel alive and now she's anything <i>but</i> alive.<br><br>How on earth did this work out so well? This author is a true genius.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2164082033793561613" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1786548126?book_show_action=true">Oct 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4725020-seffra?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4725020-seffra?shelf=the-men-i-dream-about">the-men-i-dream-about</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4725020-seffra?shelf=tortured-heroes-you-say">tortured-heroes-you-say</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4725020-seffra?shelf=best-females-ever">best-females-ever</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1786548126" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6253427435768745706">5 stars, hands down.<br/><br/> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424479789ra/13767219.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>My favourite of the series so far! I cannot get over how wonderfully beautiful Néomi and Conrad's story was. <br/><br/>Conrad was the ultimate bad guy, he was so deep into his bloodlust he was seriously scary and I didn't see how he could be redeemed. I was so wrong, his redemption was glorious as was his road to it. He was such a powerful character because of how confounding he was. He was just full of opposites and flaws that it made him such a real character and you could see his d</span>
  <span id="freeText6253427435768745706" style="display:none">5 stars, hands down.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424479789ra/13767219.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My favourite of the series so far! I cannot get over how wonderfully beautiful Néomi and Conrad's story was. <br><br>Conrad was the ultimate bad guy, he was so deep into his bloodlust he was seriously scary and I didn't see how he could be redeemed. I was so wrong, his redemption was glorious as was his road to it. He was such a powerful character because of how confounding he was. He was just full of opposites and flaws that it made him such a real character and you could see his desire for more in life and ughhhhhh.<br><br>Néomi, girl, I love you. She was so unique from Cole's other female characters because not only was she originally human before dying, she was well, a ghost. Not only physically was she different but personality wise as well. She was still strong but it was more a quiet strength that was more internal than external. She held not only herself up, but her man up and ugh, I. Love. Her.<br><br><br>So yeah, my fave from this series and it's going onto the faves shelf.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="6253427435768745706" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2434791572" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5040554268605962483">3.5 stars<br/><br/>This was my favorite in the series so far, loved the MCs with their strengths and vulnerabilities. there was no pushing away, both were all in and fought to protect each other. For the first time in the series I was really intrigued by the supernatural aspect. Maybe bc it played a big part in the relationship between our MCs, and what makes them amazing.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('77/TxjGbQ7y1X13wMoRru6RyG4mpNIl9Z/JD4UcserZrFQ7yKHtXd7HyD6tZPT2InVTp1TY1O1mVPNPWRiKDDQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('JcvnJyv+4RznDudjj3rGIdbCgTuSwJBdUuMc42aTfn+hYToTMh711+OjtTjkw5AS7+RzZw3BInmgLYzUZ52HxA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText2350545968369673538" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family.
